[2025-01-08 00:45:48,039] [DEBUG] [822][5255][com.obs.lcl.blmodule.helpers.InstaUptimeTask:1051] - with uptime_range as (
	select insta_id, 
		sum(uptime_diff)/extract(epoch from (('2025-01-08 00:45:47.772+00')::timestamptz - ('2025-01-01 00:45:47.565+00')::timestamptz)) as uptimep, 0 as cstate
	 from (select insta_id, 
		case when uptime < lag(uptime) over (partition by insta_id order by msg_ts) then uptime
		else uptime - lag(uptime) over (partition by insta_id order by msg_ts) end as uptime_diff
	from ts_var_metrics_store where insta_id=any(('{"2","3","4"}')) and msg_ts >= ('2025-01-01 00:45:47.565+00') and msg_ts < ('2025-01-08 00:45:47.772+00')) as subquery
	group by insta_id order by insta_id asc
),
current_state as (
    select insta_id, uptimep, 1 as cstate
    from (
        select insta_id, uptime as uptimep,
               row_number() over (partition by insta_id order by msg_ts desc) as rn
        from ts_var_metrics_store
    ) latest
    where rn = 1
)
select insta_id, uptimep, cstate from uptime_range
union all
select insta_id, uptimep, cstate from current_state order by insta_id

[2025-01-08 00:46:10,583] [DEBUG] [822][5271][com.obs.lcl.blmodule.helpers.InstaUptimeTask:1055] - with uptime_range as (
	select insta_id, 
		sum(uptime_diff)/extract(epoch from (('2025-01-08 00:46:10.301+00')::timestamptz - ('2024-10-25 00:45:57.476+00')::timestamptz)) as uptimep, 0 as cstate
	 from (select insta_id, 
		case when uptime < lag(uptime) over (partition by insta_id order by msg_ts) then uptime
		else uptime - lag(uptime) over (partition by insta_id order by msg_ts) end as uptime_diff
	from ts_var_metrics_store where insta_id=any(('{"2","3","4"}')) and msg_ts >= ('2024-10-25 00:45:57.476+00') and msg_ts < ('2025-01-08 00:46:10.301+00')) as subquery
	group by insta_id order by insta_id asc
),
current_state as (
    select insta_id, uptimep, 1 as cstate
    from (
        select insta_id, uptime as uptimep,
               row_number() over (partition by insta_id order by msg_ts desc) as rn
        from ts_var_metrics_store
    ) latest
    where rn = 1
)
select insta_id, uptimep, cstate from uptime_range
union all
select insta_id, uptimep, cstate from current_state order by insta_id
